h1{font-size:1rem;margin:0 0 .1rem 0;font-weight:600;letter-spacing:.02em}\n  #wrap{display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr;gap:.6rem;padding:.6rem}\n  #canvas{display:block;width:100vw;height:72vh;touch-action:none;border-bottom:1px solid #23222a}\n  .row{display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:.6rem}\n  .ctrl{display:flex;align-items:center;gap:.5rem}\n  .ctrl label{font-size:.8rem;opacity:.85;min-width:7.2rem}\n  input[type=range]{width:100%}\n  button, select{background:#181722;color:#e6e6f0;border:1px solid #2a2933;border-radius:.5rem;padding:.5rem .7rem}\n  button:hover{filter:brightness(1.1)}\n  .small{font-size:.8rem;opacity:.8}\n</style>\n</head>\n<body>\n<header>\n  <h1>Stable Fluids â€” Pocket Playground</h1>\n  <span class=\"small\">Drag to add dye & force â€¢ Works on phone</span>\n</header>\n<canvas id=\"canvas\"></canvas>\n<div id=\"wrap\">\n  <div class=\"row\">\n    <div class=\"ctrl\"><label>Grid size</label><input id=\"grid\" type=\"range\" min=\"48\" max=\"192\" step=\"16\" value=\"128\"><span id=\"gridv\">128</span></div>\n    <div class=\"ctrl\"><label>Time step</label><input id=\"dt\" type=\"range\" min=\"1\" max=\"33\" value=\"16\"><span id=\"dtv\">0.016</span></div>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"row\">\n    <div class=\"ctrl\"><label>Viscosity</label><input id=\"visc\" type=\"range\" min=\"0\" max=\"100\" value=\"3\"><span id=\"viscv\">0.003</span></div>\n    <div class=\"ctrl\"><label>Diffusion</label><input id=\"diff\" type=\"range\" min=\"0\" max=\"100\" value=\"5\"><span id=\"diffv\">0.005</span></div>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"row\">\n    <div class=\"ctrl\"><label>Brush radius</label><input id=\"brush\" type=\"range\" min=\"2\" max=\"48\" value=\"18\"><span id=\"brushv\">18</span></div>\n    <div class=\"ctrl\"><label>Force scale</label><input id=\"force\" type=\"range\" min=\"50\" max=\"2500\" value=\"1100\"><span id=\"forcev\">1100</span></div>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"row\">\n    <div class=\"ctrl\"><label>Display gain</label><input id=\"gain\" type=\"range\" min=\"10\" max=\"500\" value=\"220\"><span id=\"gainv\">2.20</span></div>\n    <div class=\"ctrl\"><label>Colormap</label>\n      <select id=\"cmap\">\n        <option value=\"neon\" selected>Neon (purpleâ†’green)</option>\n        <option value=\"gray\">Grayscale</option>\n        <option value=\"fire\">Fire</option>\n        <option value=\"ocean\">Ocean</option>\n      </select>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"row\">\n    <div class=\"ctrl\" style=\"gap:.6rem\">\n      <button id=\"reset\">Reset</button>\n      <button id=\"pause\">Pause</button>\n      <button id=\"save\">Save PNG</button>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"ctrl small\">Tip: pinch-zoom the page first, then paint. Lower grid if the phone lags.</div>\n  </div>\n</div>\n\n<script>\n/* ----------- Stable Fluids (Jos Stam) â€” CPU version, single-file ----------- */\nconst canvas = document.getElementById('canvas');\nconst ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', {alpha:false});\nlet W=canvas.clientWidth, H=canvas.clientHeight;\nfunction fitCanvas(){const dpr=window.devicePixelRatio||1; W=canvas.clientWidth; H=canvas.clientHeight; canvas.width=W*dpr; canvas.height=H*dpr; ctx.setTransform(dpr,0,0,dpr,0,0);}\nfitCanvas(); addEventListener('resize', fitCanvas);\n\n// UI\nconst ui = (id)=>document.getElementById(id);\nconst grid=ui('grid'), dtUI=ui('dt'), viscUI=ui('visc'), diffUI=ui('diff'), brushUI=ui('brush'), forceUI=ui('force'), gainUI=ui('gain');\nconst gridV=ui('gridv'), dtV=ui('dtv'), viscV=ui('viscv'), diffV=ui('diffv'), brushV=ui('brushv'), forceV=ui('forcev'), gainV=ui('gainv');\nconst cmapSel=ui('cmap'); const resetBtn=ui('reset'), pauseBtn=ui('pause'), saveBtn=ui('save');\nlet paused=false;\n\n// Helpers\nfunction clamp(x,a,b){return x<a?a:x>b?b:x;}\nfunction idx(x,y){return x + N * y;}\n\n// Simulation state\nlet N = parseInt(grid.value);\nlet size = (N+2)*(N+2);\nlet dens, densPrev, u, v, uPrev, vPrev;\nfunction alloc(){\n  size = (N+2)*(N+2);\n  dens=new Float32Array(size); densPrev=new Float32Array(size);\n  u=new Float32Array(size); v=new Float32Array(size);\n  uPrev=new Float32Array(size); vPrev=new Float32Array(size);\n}\nalloc();\n\nfunction set_bnd(b, x){\n  for(let i=1;i<=N;i++){\n    x[idx(0,i)]     = b===1 ? -x[idx(1,i)] : x[idx(1,i)];\n    x[idx(N+1,i)]   = b===1 ? -x[idx(N,i)] : x[idx(N,i)];\n    x[idx(i,0)]     = b===2 ? -x[idx(i,1)] : x[idx(i,1)];\n    x[idx(i,N+1)]   = b===2 ? -x[idx(i,N)] : x[idx(i,N)];\n  }\n  x[idx(0,0)]       = 0.5*(x[idx(1,0)]+x[idx(0,1)]);\n  x[idx(0,N+1)]     = 0.5*(x[idx(1,N+1)]+x[idx(0,N)]);\n  x[idx(N+1,0)]     = 0.5*(x[idx(N,0)]+x[idx(N+1,1)]);\n  x[idx(N+1,N+1)]   = 0.5*(x[idx(N,N+1)]+x[idx(N+1,N)]);\n}\n\nfunction lin_solve(b, x, x0, a, c){\n  for(let k=0;k<20;k++){\n    for(let j=1;j<=N;j++){\n      for(let i=1;i<=N;i++){\n        x[idx(i,j)] = (x0[idx(i,j)] + a*(x[idx(i-1,j)] + x[idx(i+1,j)] + x[idx(i,j-1)] + x[idx(i,j+1)]))/c;\n      }\n    }\n    set_bnd(b,x);\n  }\n}\nfunction diffuse(b, x, x0, diff, dt){\n  const a = dt*diff*N*N;\n  lin_solve(b,x,x0,a,1+4*a);\n}\nfunction advect(b, d, d0, u, v, dt){\n  const dt0 = dt*N;\n  for(let j=1;j<=N;j++){\n    for(let i=1;i<=N;i++){\n      let x = i - dt0*u[idx(i,j)];\n      let y = j - dt0*v[idx(i,j)];\n      if(x<0.5) x=0.5; if(x>N+0.5) x=N+0.5;\n      if(y<0.5) y=0.5; if(y>N+0.5) y=N+0.5;\n      let i0=Math.floor(x), i1=i0+1;\n      let j0=Math.floor(y), j1=j0+1;\n      let s1=x-i0, s0=1-s1, t1=y-j0, t0=1-t1;\n      d[idx(i,j)] =\n        s0*(t0*d0[idx(i0,j0)] + t1*d0[idx(i0,j1)]) +\n        s1*(t0*d0[idx(i1,j0)] + t1*d0[idx(i1,j1)]);\n    }\n  }\n  set_bnd(b,d);\n}\nfunction project(u,v,p,div){\n  for(let j=1;j<=N;j++){\n    for(let i=1;i<=N;i++){\n      div[idx(i,j)] = -0.5*(u[idx(i+1,j)]-u[idx(i-1,j)] + v[idx(i,j+1)]-v[idx(i,j-1)]) / N;\n      p[idx(i,j)] = 0;\n    }\n  }\n  set_bnd(0,div); set_bnd(0,p);\n  lin_solve(0,p,div,1,4);\n  for(let j=1;j<=N;j++){\n    for(let i=1;i<=N;i++){\n      u[idx(i,j)] -= 0.5*N*(p[idx(i+1,j)]-p[idx(i-1,j)]);\n      v[idx(i,j)] -= 0.5*N*(p[idx(i,j+1)]-p[idx(i,j-1)]);\n    }\n  }\n  set_bnd(1,u); set_bnd(2,v);\n}\n\nfunction addSource(x, s, dt){\n  for(let i=0;i<size;i++) x[i] += dt*s[i];\n}\n\nfunction vel_step(u,v,u0,v0,visc,dt){\n  addSource(u,u0,dt); addSource(v,v0,dt);\n  [u0,u] = [u,u0]; diffuse(1,u,u0,visc,dt);\n  [v0,v] = [v,v0]; diffuse(2,v,v0,visc,dt);\n  project(u,v,u0,v0);\n  [u0,u] = [u,u0]; [v0,v] = [v,v0];\n  advect(1,u,u0,u0,v0,dt);\n  advect(2,v,v0,u0,v0,dt);\n  project(u,v,u0,v0);\n}\nfunction dens_step(x, x0, u, v, diff, dt){\n  addSource(x,x0,dt);\n  [x0,x] = [x,x0]; diffuse(0,x,x0,diff,dt);\n  [x0,x] = [x,x0]; advect(0,x,x0,u,v,dt);\n}\n\n// Painting\nlet painting=false, lastX=0, lastY=0;\nfunction toGrid(px,py){\n  const r = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();\n  const x = (px - r.left)/r.width, y=(py - r.top)/r.height;\n  const gx = Math.floor(clamp(1 + x*N, 1, N));\n  const gy = Math.floor(clamp(1 + y*N, 1, N));\n  return {gx, gy};\n}\nfunction addBrush(x,y,dx,dy){\n  const rad = parseInt(brushUI.value);\n  const fscale = parseFloat(forceUI.value);\n  for(let j=-rad;j<=rad;j++){\n    for(let i=-rad;i<=rad;i++){\n      const xi = x+i, yj = y+j;\n      if(xi<1||xi>N||yj<1||yj>N) continue;\n      const d2 = i*i + j*j;\n      if(d2<=rad*rad){\n        const id = idx(xi,yj);\n        densPrev[id] += 50; // dye impulse\n        uPrev[id] += dx * fscale / (d2+10);\n        vPrev[id] += dy * fscale / (d2+10);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\nfunction pointerDown(e){\n  e.preventDefault(); painting=true;\n  const p = e.touches? e.touches[0] : e;\n  const g = toGrid(p.clientX, p.clientY); lastX=g.gx; lastY=g.gy;\n}\nfunction pointerMove(e){\n  if(!painting) return;\n  const p = e.touches? e.touches[0] : e;\n  const g = toGrid(p.clientX, p.clientY);\n  const dx = g.gx - lastX, dy = g.gy - lastY;\n  addBrush(g.gx,g.gy,dx,dy);\n  lastX=g.gx; lastY=g.gy;\n}\nfunction pointerUp(){painting=false;}\ncanvas.addEventListener('pointerdown', (e)=>{pointerDown(e);});\ncanvas.addEventListener('pointermove', pointerMove);\ncanvas.addEventListener('pointerup', pointerUp);\ncanvas.addEventListener('pointercancel', pointerUp);\ncanvas.addEventListener('pointerout', pointerUp);\ncanvas.addEventListener('touchstart', pointerDown, {passive:false});\ncanvas.addEventListener('touchmove', pointerMove, {passive:false});\ncanvas.addEventListener('touchend', pointerUp);\n\n// Rendering\nfunction hsv2rgb(h,s,v){\n  let c=v*s, x=c*(1-Math.abs((h/60)%2-1)), m=v-c, r=0,g=0,b=0;\n  if(h<60){r=c;g=x;} else if(h<120){r=x;g=c;}\n  else if(h<180){g=c;b=x;} else if(h<240){g=x;b=c;}\n  else if(h<300){r=x;b=c;} else {r=c;b=x;}\n  return [(r+m)*255,(g+m)*255,(b+m)*255];\n}\nfunction colorMap(d,t){\n  d = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, d));\n  if(t==='gray'){ const v = Math.pow(d,0.6)*255; return [v,v,v]; }\n  if(t==='fire'){ const h = 10 + 60*(1-d); return hsv2rgb(h,1,Math.pow(d,0.7)); }\n  if(t==='ocean'){ const h = 180 + 90*(1-d); return hsv2rgb(h,0.8,Math.pow(d,0.7)); }\n  // neon: purple background to green/yellow hotspots\n  const h = 290 - 240*Math.pow(d,0.5); // 290â†’50\n  const s = 1.0, v = Math.pow(d,0.9)*1.0;\n  return hsv2rgb(h,s,Math.max(0.2,v));\n}\n\nfunction render(){\n  const img = ctx.createImageData(W, H);\n  const gain = parseFloat(gainUI.value)/100;\n  for(let y=0;y<H;y++){\n    const gy = 1 + Math.floor(y/H*N);\n    for(let x=0;x<W;x++){\n      const gx = 1 + Math.floor(x/W*N);\n      const d = dens[idx(gx,gy)] * 0.0035 * gain;\n      const [r,g,b] = colorMap(d, cmapSel.value);\n      const k = (x + y*W)*4;\n      img.data[k]=r; img.data[k+1]=g; img.data[k+2]=b; img.data[k+3]=255;\n    }\n  }\n  ctx.putImageData(img,0,0);\n}\n\n// Main loop\nfunction clearPrev(){ uPrev.fill(0); vPrev.fill(0); densPrev.fill(0); }\nfunction step(){\n  const dt = parseInt(dtUI.value)/1000;\n  const visc = parseInt(viscUI.value)/1000;\n  const diff = parseInt(diffUI.value)/1000;\n  vel_step(u,v,uPrev,vPrev,visc,dt);\n  dens_step(dens,densPrev,u,v,diff,dt);\n  clearPrev();\n}\nfunction loop(){\n  if(!paused) step();\n  render();\n  requestAnimationFrame(loop);\n}\nloop();\n\n// UI interactions\nfunction refreshLabels(){\n  gridV.textContent = N.toString();\n  dtV.textContent = (parseInt(dtUI.value)/1000).toFixed(3);\n  viscV.textContent = (parseInt(viscUI.value)/1000).toFixed(3);\n  diffV.textContent = (parseInt(diffUI.value)/1000).toFixed(3);\n  brushV.textContent = brushUI.value;\n  forceV.textContent = forceUI.value;\n  gainV.textContent = (parseInt(gainUI.value)/100).toFixed(2);\n}\nrefreshLabels();\n[grid,dtUI,viscUI,diffUI,brushUI,forceUI,gainUI,cmapSel].forEach(el=>{\n  el.addEventListener('input', ()=>{\n    if(el===grid){\n      N=parseInt(grid.value); alloc();\n    }\n    refreshLabels();\n  });\n});\nresetBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{ alloc(); });\npauseBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{ paused=!paused; pauseBtn.textContent = paused? 'Resume':'Pause'; });\nsaveBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{\n  const link = document.createElement('a');\n  link.download = 'fluid.png';\n  link.href = canvas.toDataURL('image/png');\n  link.click();\n});\n</script>\n</body>\n</html>\n\"\"\"\n\nwith open('/mnt/data/phone_fluid.html', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n    f.write(html)\n\n'/mnt/data/phone_fluid.html'\n```\n\nResult\n\nundefined\n\nHell yes. Letâ€™s go through both carefully:\n\n* * *\n\nğŸ§ª Part 1: **Why is the octet rule a thing? What makes â€œ8â€ special?**\n---------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n### TL;DR:\n\nThe â€œoctet ruleâ€ arises from the **quantum mechanical structure of atomic orbitals**, particularly the way **electrons fill energy levels** based on **Pauli exclusion, spin, and orbital degeneracy**. The magic number 8 comes from:\n\n*   2 electrons in the **s-orbital** (1 orbital Ã— 2 spins)\n*   6 electrons in the **p-orbitals** (3 orbitals Ã— 2 spins)\n*   â†’ total of 8 in the **n=2** shell (2s + 2p), which is the first full valence shell with both s and p available.\n\n### Deep Dive:\n\n1.  **Quantum numbers determine orbital structure**  \n    Every electron in an atom is described by four quantum numbers:\n    *   `n` (principal energy level)\n    *   `l` (angular momentum, defines orbital shape)\n    *   `m_l` (orbital orientation)\n    *   `m_s` (spin: Â±Â½)\n2.  **Each orbital holds 2 electrons** due to the Pauli exclusion principle: no two electrons can share the same set of all four quantum numbers.  \n    So:\n    *   1s: 2 electrons\n    *   2s: 2 electrons\n    *   2p (three p orbitals): 6 electrons  \n        â†’ Total: **8 electrons in 2nd shell** = â€œoctetâ€\n3.  **Why stop at 8?**  \n    You donâ€™t, really. Once you get to d and f orbitals, things get more complex, but in organic chemistry and the periodic tableâ€™s left-to-right \"chemically active\" zone (Groups Iâ€“VIII), the octet is _really_ predictive.\n4.  **Energetic stability of filled shells:**  \n    Filled shells (especially filled s and p) have **spherically symmetric, low-energy distributions**, minimizing electron repulsion and maximizing nuclear attraction.
